                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>গ্যাস অণুর আকার যত বড় হয় 'a' মান তত বেশি হয়।<br>

[হাজারী স্যার: সংস্করণ-২০২২, পৃষ্ঠা-৫১]</p>

font-family: MathJax_Main;">×</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-59" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">1</span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.445em, 1001.03em, 4.141em, -999.998em); top: -3.645em; left: 50%; margin-left: -0.531em;"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-60" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">125</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(0.904em, 1002.09em, 1.191em, -999.998em); top: -1.268em; left: 0em;"><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; [হাজারী স্যার: সংস্করণ-২০২২, পৃষ্ঠা-১২]</p>

                                    <div class="row solveText" style="display: block; padding:10px; color:#077307; overflow-x: auto; background-color: #d7f7d4;">
                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>কক্ষ তাপমাত্রায় অক্সিজেন, নাইট্রোজেন গ্যাসের অণুসমূহের বর্গমূল গড়-বর্গ গতিবেগ প্রায় <span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit; =1000\ cm^3 </script></span><br>

                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>

                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>n মোল গ্যাস অণুর গড় গতিশক্তি =&nbsp;<span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit; display: none;"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-69-Frame" tabindex="0" style="position: relative;" data-mathml="<math xmlns=&quot;http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML&quot;><mfrac><mrow><mn>3</mn><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>n</mi><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>R</mi><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>T</mi></mrow><mn>2</mn></mfrac></math>" role="presentation"><nobr aria-hidden="true"><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-881" style="width: 2.174em; 64&nbsp;g অক্সিজেন = <span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit; display: none;"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-70-Frame" tabindex="0" style="position: relative;" data-mathml="<math xmlns=&quot;http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML&quot;><mfrac><mn>64</mn><mn>32</mn></mfrac><mo>=</mo><mn>2</mn></math>" role="presentation"><nobr aria-hidden="true"><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-890" style="width: 2.953em; <span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit; display: none;"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-71-Frame" tabindex="0" style="position: relative;" data-mathml="<math xmlns=&quot;http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML&quot;><mo>&amp;#x2234;</mo></math>" role="presentation"><nobr aria-hidden="true"><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-897" style="width: 0.658em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 0.535em; height: 0px; font-size: 122%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.641em, 1000.49em, 2.42em, -999.998em); top: -2.211em; left: 0em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-898"><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-899" style="font-family: MathJax_AMS;">∴</span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.215em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.148em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 0.753em;"></span></span></nobr><span class="MJX_Assistive_MathML" role="presentation"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mo>∴</mo></math></span></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-71">\therefore</script></span> 2 মোল গ্যাস অণুর গড় গতিশক্তি 3RT<br>

                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>(i) NaOH -এর অম্লত্ব 1<br>
(ii) CaO -এর অম্লত্ব 2<br>

                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
